# Fix Memory Leak in Dynamic Forward Proxy Cluster

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/envoy--5160151e (mirror of envoyproxy/envoy)
**Difficulty:** HARD
**Category:** cross_module_bug_fix

## Description

Envoy's Dynamic Forward Proxy (DFP) cluster has a memory leak that occurs when a host's DNS resolution changes to a new IP address. When a DFP host initially resolves to IP address A, a `LogicalHost` is created and added to both the `host_map_` and the cross-priority host map (tracked by `MainPrioritySetImpl`). When the same host later re-resolves to IP address B, the current code updates the `LogicalHost`'s address in-place via `setNewAddresses()` without removing the old address from the cross-priority host map.

This means IP A remains in the cross-priority host map permanently. When the host's TTL expires and it is removed, only IP B is cleaned up from the map — IP A leaks. Over time, with repeated DNS re-resolution, the cross-priority host map grows without bound.

The fix refactors `addOrUpdateHost()` to remove the old host and create a new `LogicalHost` with the new address, properly emitting both `hosts_added` and `hosts_removed` events to the priority set. The method signature is simplified to remove the accumulated `hosts_added` vector pattern, and `updatePriorityState()` is called directly within `addOrUpdateHost()`. Debug logging is also added to `upstream_impl.cc` for cross-priority host map operations.

## Task

Changes:
- 4 files modified (upstream_impl.cc, cluster.cc, cluster.h, cluster_test.cc)
- 29 additions, 39 deletions

Tasks:
1. Add debug logging to `source/common/upstream/upstream_impl.cc` for cross-priority host map mutations
2. Refactor `addOrUpdateHost()` in `source/extensions/clusters/dynamic_forward_proxy/cluster.cc` to replace in-place address updates with host removal and re-creation
3. Simplify the `addOrUpdateHost()` signature in `cluster.h` (remove the `hosts_added` out-parameter)
4. Update test expectations in `cluster_test.cc` for the new per-host update notification pattern

## Success Criteria

Code changes match the expected ground-truth fix.
Code follows repository conventions.
No regressions in existing functionality.
All 4 modified files updated correctly.

HostMapConstSharedPtr MainPrioritySetImpl::crossPriorityHostMap() const {
  // Check if the host set in the main thread PrioritySet has been updated.
  if (mutable_cross_priority_host_map_ != nullptr) {
    const_cross_priority_host_map_ = std::move(mutable_cross_priority_host_map_);
    ASSERT(mutable_cross_priority_host_map_ == nullptr);
  }
  return const_cross_priority_host_map_;
}

void MainPrioritySetImpl::updateCrossPriorityHostMap(const HostVector& hosts_added,
                                                     const HostVector& hosts_removed) {
  if (hosts_added.empty() && hosts_removed.empty()) {
    // No new hosts have been added and no old hosts have been removed.
    return;
  }

  // Since read_only_all_host_map_ may be shared by multiple threads, when the host set changes,
  // we cannot directly modify read_only_all_host_map_.
  if (mutable_cross_priority_host_map_ == nullptr) {
    // Copy old read only host map to mutable host map.
    mutable_cross_priority_host_map_ = std::make_shared<HostMap>(*const_cross_priority_host_map_);
  }

  ENVOY_LOG(debug, "Removing hosts from cross-priority host map");
  for (const auto& host : hosts_removed) {
    ENVOY_LOG(debug, "Removing host from cross-priority host map: {}", addressToString(host->address()));
    mutable_cross_priority_host_map_->erase(addressToString(host->address()));
  }

  ENVOY_LOG(debug, "Adding hosts to cross-priority host map");
  for (const auto& host : hosts_added) {
    ENVOY_LOG(debug, "Adding host to cross-priority host map: {}", addressToString(host->address()));
    mutable_cross_priority_host_map_->insert({addressToString(host->address()), host});
  }
}

  for (const auto& host : host_map_) {\n        cb(host.first, host.second);\n      }\n    }));\n    if (!existing_hosts.empty()) {\n      EXPECT_CALL(*this, onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(existing_hosts.size()), SizeIs(0)));\n    }\n    cluster_->initialize([] {});\n  }\n\n  Extensions::Common::DynamicForwardProxy::DnsCacheManagerSharedPtr get() override {\n    return dns_cache_manager_;\n  }\n\n  void makeTestHost(const std::string& host, const std::string& address) {\n    EXPECT_TRUE(host_map_.find(host) == host_map_.end());\n    host_map_[host] = std::make_shared<Extensions::Common::DynamicForwardProxy::MockDnsHostInfo>();\n    host_map_[host]->address_ = Network::Utility::parseInternetAddress(address);\n\n    // Allow touch() to still be strict.\n    EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[host], address()).Times(AtLeast(0));\n    EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[host], addressList()).Times(AtLeast(0));\n    EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[host], EXPECT_FALSE(host_map_.find(host) == host_map_.end());\n    host_map_[host]->address_ = Network::Utility::parseInternetAddress(address);\n  }\n\n  void refreshLb() { lb_ = lb_factory_->create(lb_params_); }\n\n  Upstream::MockLoadBalancerContext* setHostAndReturnContext(const std::string& host) {\n    downstream_headers_.remove(\":authority\");\n StreamInfo::StreamSharingMayImpactPooling::SharedWithUpstreamConnection);\n\n    return &lb_context_;\n  }\n\n  void setOutlierFailed(const std::string& host) {\n    for (auto& h : cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts()) {\n      if (h->hostname() == host) {\n        h->healthFlagSet(Upstream::Host::HealthFlag::FAILED_OUTLIER_CHECK);\n        break;\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  void clearOutlierFailed(const std::string& host) {\n    for (auto& h : cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts()) {\n      if (h->hostname() == host) {\n        h->healthFlagClear(Upstream::Host::HealthFlag::FAILED_OUTLIER_CHECK);\n        break;\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  MOCK_METHOD(void, onMemberUpdateCb,\n              (const Upstream::HostVector& \"fake_cluster_name\";\n  const std::string host = \"localhost\";\n  const int port = 80;\n  std::pair<bool, absl::optional<envoy::config::cluster::v3::Cluster>> sub_cluster_pair =\n      cluster_->createSubClusterConfig(cluster_name, host, port);\n  EXPECT_EQ(true, sub_cluster_pair.first);\n  EXPECT_EQ(true, sub_cluster_pair.second.has_value());\n\n  // create again, already exists\n of the cluster including adding hosts and removing them.\nTEST_F(ClusterTest, BasicFlow) {\n  initialize(default_yaml_config_, false);\n  makeTestHost(\"host1:0\", \"1.2.3.4\");\n  InSequence s;\n\n  EXPECT_EQ(nullptr, lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"\")));\n\n  // Verify no host LB cases.\n  EXPECT_EQ(nullptr, lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"foo\")));\n  EXPECT_EQ(nullptr, lb_->peekAnotherHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"foo\")));\n\n  // LB will immediately resolve host1.\n  EXPECT_CALL(*this, onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(1), SizeIs(0)));\n  update_callbacks_->onDnsHostAddOrUpdate(\"host1:0\", host_map_[\"host1:0\"]);\n  EXPECT_EQ(1UL, cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts().size());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"1.2.3.4:0\",\n            cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts()[0]->address()->asString());\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host1:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"1.2.3.4:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\"))->address()->asString());\n\n  // After changing the address, LB will immediately resolve the new address with a refresh.\n  updateTestHostAddress(\"host1:0\", \"2.3.4.5\");\n  EXPECT_CALL(*this, onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(1), SizeIs(1)));\n  update_callbacks_->onDnsHostAddOrUpdate(\"host1:0\", host_map_[\"host1:0\"]);\n  EXPECT_EQ(1UL, cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts().size());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"2.3.4.5:0\",\n            cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts()[0]->address()->asString());\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host1:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"2.3.4.5:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\"))->address()->asString());\n\n  // Remove the host, LB will immediately fail to find the host in the map.\n  EXPECT_CALL(*this, onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(0), SizeIs(1)));\n  update_callbacks_->onDnsHostRemove(\"host1:0\");\n  EXPECT_EQ(0UL, cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts().size());\n  EXPECT_EQ(nullptr, lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\")));\n}\n\n// Outlier detection\nTEST_F(ClusterTest, OutlierDetection) {\n  initialize(default_yaml_config_, false);\n  makeTestHost(\"host1:0\", \"1.2.3.4\");\n  makeTestHost(\"host2:0\", \"5.6.7.8\");\n  InSequence s;\n\n  EXPECT_CALL(*this, onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(1), SizeIs(0)));\n  update_callbacks_->onDnsHostAddOrUpdate(\"host1:0\", host_map_[\"host1:0\"]);\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host1:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"1.2.3.4:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\"))->address()->asString());\n\n  EXPECT_CALL(*this, onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(1), SizeIs(0)));\n  update_callbacks_->onDnsHostAddOrUpdate(\"host2:0\", host_map_[\"host2:0\"]);\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host2:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"5.6.7.8:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host2:0\"))->address()->asString());\n\n  // Fail outlier check for host1\n  setOutlierFailed(\"host1:0\");\n  EXPECT_EQ(nullptr, lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\")));\n  // \"host2:0\" should not be affected\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host2:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"5.6.7.8:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host2:0\"))->address()->asString());\n\n  // Clear outlier check failure for host1, it should be available again\n  clearOutlierFailed(\"host1:0\");\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host1:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"1.2.3.4:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\"))->address()->asString());\n}\n\n// Various invalid LB   "new_string": "void Cluster::addOrUpdateHost(\n    absl::string_view host,\n    const Extensions::Common::DynamicForwardProxy::DnsHostInfoSharedPtr& host_info) {\n  Upstream::HostVector hosts_added;\n  Upstream::HostVector hosts_removed;\n  {\n    absl::WriterMutexLock lock{&host_map_lock_};\n\n    // NOTE: Right now we allow a DNS cache to be shared between multiple clusters. Though we have\n    // connection/request circuit breakers on the cluster, we don't have any way to control the\n    // maximum hosts on a cluster. We currently assume that host data shared via shared pointer is\n    // a marginal memory cost above that already used by connections and requests, so relying on\n    // connection/request circuit breakers is sufficient. We may have to revisit this in the\n    // future.\n    const auto host_map_it = host_map_.find(host);\n    if (host_map_it != host_map_.end()) {\n      // If we have an address change, remove the old host and create a new one.\n      // This ensures proper updates to the cross-priority host map.\n      ASSERT(host_info == host_map_it->second.shared_host_info_);\n      if (host_map_it->second.shared_host_info_->address() !=\n          host_map_it->second.logical_host_->address()) {\n        ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"updating dfproxy cluster host address '{}'\", host);\n        // Collect the old host for removal\n        hosts_removed.emplace_back(host_map_it->second.logical_host_);\n        host_map_.erase(host_map_it);\n\n        // Create a new host with the updated address\n        auto emplaced_host =\n            host_map_\n                .try_emplace(host, host_info,\n                             std::make_shared<Upstream::LogicalHost>(\n                                 info(), std::string{host}, host_info->address(),\n                                 host_info->addressList(), dummy_locality_lb_endpoint_,\n                                 dummy_lb_endpoint_, nullptr, time_source_))\n                .first->second.logical_host_;\n        hosts_added.emplace_back(emplaced_host);\n        // Unlock before calling updatePriorityState to avoid deadlock\n      }\n      // If address didn't change, do nothing\n      if (hosts_added.empty() && hosts_removed.empty()) {\n        return;\n      }\n    } else {\n      ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"adding new dfproxy cluster host '{}'\", host);\n\n      auto emplaced_host = host_map_\n                               .try_emplace(host, host_info,\n Though we have\n    // connection/request circuit breakers on the cluster, we don't have any way to control the\n    // maximum hosts on a cluster. We currently assume that host data shared via shared pointer is\n    // a marginal memory cost above that already used by connections and requests, so relying on\n    // connection/request circuit breakers is sufficient. dummy_lb_endpoint_, nullptr, time_source_))\n                .first->second.logical_host_;\n        hosts_added.emplace_back(emplaced_host);\n      }\n      // If address didn't change, do nothing\n      if (hosts_added.empty() && hosts_removed.empty()) {\n        return;\n      }\n    } else {\n      ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"adding new dfproxy cluster host '{}'\", host);\n\n      auto emplaced_host = Before
void Cluster::startPreInit() {
  // If we are attaching to a pre-populated cache we need to initialize our hosts.
  std::unique_ptr<Upstream::HostVector> hosts_added;
  dns_cache_->iterateHostMap(
      [&](absl::string_view host, const Common::DynamicForwardProxy::DnsHostInfoSharedPtr& info) {
        addOrUpdateHost(host, info);
        // Collect the hosts that were added
        {
          absl::ReaderMutexLock lock{&host_map_lock_};
          const auto host_map_it = host_map_.find(host);
          if (host_map_it != host_map_.end()) {
            if (hosts_added == nullptr) {
              hosts_added = std::make_unique<Upstream::HostVector>();
            }
            hosts_added->emplace_back(host_map_it->second.logical_host_);
          }
        }
      });
  if (hosts_added) {
    updatePriorityState(*hosts_added, {});
  }
  onPreInitComplete();
}
After

5. EDIT /workspace/source/extensions/clusters/dynamic_forward_proxy/cluster.cc
Before
void Cluster::addOrUpdateHost(
    absl::string_view host,
    const Extensions::Common::DynamicForwardProxy::DnsHostInfoSharedPtr& host_info) {
  Upstream::HostVector hosts_added;
  Upstream::HostVector hosts_removed;
  {
    absl::WriterMutexLock lock{&host_map_lock_};

    // NOTE: Right now we allow a DNS cache to be shared between multiple clusters. Though we have
    // connection/request circuit breakers on the cluster, we don't have any way to control the
    // maximum hosts on a cluster. We currently assume that host data shared via shared pointer is
    // a marginal memory cost above that already used by connections and requests, so relying on
    // connection/request circuit breakers is sufficient. We may have to revisit this in the
    // future.
    const auto host_map_it = host_map_.find(host);
    if (host_map_it != host_map_.end()) {
      // If we have an address change, remove the old host and create a new one.
      // This ensures proper updates to the cross-priority host map.
      ASSERT(host_info == host_map_it->second.shared_host_info_);
      if (host_map_it->second.shared_host_info_->address() !=
          host_map_it->second.logical_host_->address()) {
        ENVOY_LOG(debug, "updating dfproxy cluster host address '{}'", host);
        // Collect the old host for removal
        hosts_removed.emplace_back(host_map_it->second.logical_host_);
        host_map_.erase(host_map_it);

        // Create a new host with the updated address
        auto emplaced_host =
            host_map_
                .try_emplace(host, host_info,
                             std::make_shared<Upstream::LogicalHost>(
                                 info(), std::string{host}, host_info->address(),
                                 host_info->addressList(), dummy

After
void Cluster::startPreInit() {
  // If we are attaching to a pre-populated cache we need to initialize our hosts.
  dns_cache_->iterateHostMap(
      [&](absl::string_view host, const Common::DynamicForwardProxy::DnsHostInfoSharedPtr& info) {
        addOrUpdateHost(host, info);
      });
  // Collect all hosts that were added during initialization
  Upstream::HostVector hosts_added;
  {
    absl::ReaderMutexLock lock{&host_map_lock_};
    for (const auto& host : host_map_) {
      hosts_added.emplace_back(host.second.logical_host_);
    }
  }
  if (!hosts_added.empty()) {
    updatePriorityState(hosts_added, {});
  }
  onPreInitComplete();
}

      hosts_added.emplace_back(host.second.logical_host_);
    }
  }
  if (!hosts_added.empty()) {
    updatePriorityState(hosts_added, {});
  }
  onPreInitComplete();
}
After
void Cluster::startPreInit() {
  // If we are attaching to a pre-populated cache we need to initialize our hosts.
  dns_cache_->iterateHostMap(
      [&](absl::string_view host, const Common::DynamicForwardProxy::DnsHostInfoSharedPtr& info) {
        addOrUpdateHost(host, info);
      });
  // Collect all hosts that were added during initialization
  Upstream::HostVector hosts_added;
  {
    absl::ReaderMutexLock lock{&host_map_lock_};
    for (const auto& host : host_map_) {
      hosts_added.emplace_back(host.second.logical_host_);
    }
  }
  if (!hosts_added.empty()) {
    updatePriorityState(hosts_added, {});
  }
  // Mark initialization as complete
  initializing_ = false;
  onPreInitComplete();
}
9. EDIT /workspace/source/extensions/clusters/dynamic_forward_proxy/cluster.cc
Before
void Cluster::addOrUpdateHost(
    absl::string_view host,
    const Extensions::Common::DynamicForwardProxy::DnsHostInfoSharedPtr& host_info) {
  Upstream::HostVector hosts_added;
  Upstream::HostVector hosts_removed;
  {
    absl::WriterMutexLock lock{&host_map_lock_};

    // NOTE: Right now we allow a DNS cache to be shared between multiple clusters. Though we have
    // connection/request circuit breakers on the cluster, we don't have any way to control the
    // maximum hosts on a cluster. We currently assume that host data shared via shared pointer is
    // a marginal memory cost above that already used by connections and requests, so relying on
    // connection/request circuit breakers is sufficient. We may have to revisit this in the
    // future.
    const auto host_map_it = host_map_.find(host);
    if (host_map_it != host_map_.end()) {
      // If we have an address change, remove the old host and create a new one.
      // This ensures proper updates to the cross-priority host map.
      ASSERT(host_info == host_map_it->second.shared_host_info_);
      if (host_map_it->second.shared_host_info_->address() !=
          host_map_it->second.logical_host_->address()) {
        ENVOY_LOG(debug, "updating dfproxy cluster host address '{}'", host);
        // Collect the old host for removal
        hosts_removed.emplace_back(host_map_it->second.logical_host_);
        host_map_.erase(host_map_it);

        // Create a new host with the updated address
        auto emplaced_host =
            host_map_
                .try_emplace(host, host_info,
                             std::make_shared<Upstream::LogicalHost>(
                                 info(), std::string{host}, host_info->address(),
                                 host_info->addressList(), dummy
... (truncated)
